PLAN:
  === ADJUSTED ENVIRONMENT SETUP PLAN (for x86_64, Ubuntu 22.04, No GPU, WORKDIR: /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest) ===
  **Key Adjustments:**
  - All instructions and paths are aligned for Ubuntu 22.04 on x86_64 (amd64).
  - No GPU/CUDA components or drivers are included.
  - All images, binaries, and tools explicitly selected for x86_64/amd64.
  - WORKDIR is set to `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`.
  - Shell/Bash script usage assumes a Linux (Ubuntu) shell.
  - Emphasize local system setup; Docker-specific notes included where relevant.
  - Paths are all Linux-style (`/`), and file permissions commands are included where relevant.
  - Storage and memory requirements are flagged for user review, but not explicitly set due to lack of provided resource limits.
  ---
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED: 
     - **GraalVM (Java 17, version 17.0.7-graal, x86_64/amd64 Linux)**
       - Required for glue code integration and GraalPython.
       - Install via SDKMAN! (recommended, works natively on Ubuntu 22.04 x86_64).
       - Do not use ARM or other architectures.
     - **SDKMAN!**
       - Tool to install/manage GraalVM.
       - Install per https://sdkman.io/install (works on Ubuntu 22.04).
     - **GraalVM Python Component**
       - Install using `gu install python` after GraalVM is set up.
     - **Maven**
       - Required to build and test Java projects.
       - Use Ubuntu package manager (`apt install maven`) or download from https://maven.apache.org/download.html.
       - Ensure version is compatible with Java 17 (Ubuntu 22.04 default is Maven 3.6+).
     - **Python 3.11.4 (x86_64, Ubuntu)**
       - For running translated Python tests/scripts.
       - Use `pyenv` or official installer (recommended: `pyenv install 3.11.4`).
     - **pip**
       - Should come with Python install.
     - **pytest (latest stable)**
       - Install via `pip install pytest`.
     - **Other Python dependencies**
       - Check for requirements.txt or audit scripts, add as needed.
     - **Git**
       - For version control. Install via `sudo apt install git` if needed.
     - **Bash Shell**
       - Native on Ubuntu; all shell scripts will run without issue.
     - **(Optional) Docker**
       - Since Docker 28.3.2 is available, optional for containerized builds. Use only amd64-compatible base images (e.g., `ubuntu:22.04`, `python:3.11-slim`, etc.). Do not use any ARM or GPU-specific tags.

     - **Original Java Unit Tests**

       - Ensure `scripts/generate_glue.py` works as intended.

       - Ensure `scripts/clients/selenium.py` and `scripts/clients/bash_script_version.sh` run on Ubuntu and output data correctly.
  4. COMPLETE TODO LIST: 
     1. **Install SDKMAN!**
        - Run: `curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash`
        - After install, restart the shell or source profile.
        - Verify: `sdk version`
     2. **Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal, x86_64)**
        - Run: `sdk install java 17.0.7-graal`
        - Verify: `java -version` (should show GraalVM, version 17.0.7, x86_64)
        - If version not found, use `sdk list java` to choose the closest supported GraalVM 17 x86_64.
     3. **Install GraalVM Python Component**
        - Run: `gu install python`
        - Verify: `graalpython --version`
     4. **Install Maven**
        - Recommended: `sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install maven`
        - Verify: `mvn -v`
     5. **Install Python 3.11.4**
        - Install pyenv: `curl https://pyenv.run | bash`
        - Install Python: `pyenv install 3.11.4`
        - Set local version: `pyenv local 3.11.4`
        - If pyenv not preferred, use deadsnakes PPA or download from python.org binaries for x86_64.
        - Verify: `python --version`
     6. **Set Up Python Virtual Environment**
        - Run: `python -m venv venv`
        - Activate: `. venv/bin/activate`
        - Verify: Shell prompt shows `(venv)`
     7. **Install Python Dependencies**
        - Update/create `requirements.txt` as needed.
        - Run: `pip install -r requirements.txt`
        - Verify: `pytest --version`
     8. **Clone/Download Project Repository**
        - `git clone <repo-url> /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`
        - Verify folders: `commons-cli`, `commons-csv`, etc.
     9. **Create/Review Configuration Files**
        - Ensure existence and correctness of `.gitignore`, `requirements.txt`, `.env.example`, and `README.local.md`.
     10. **Run Java Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - Verify: All tests pass.
     11. **Run Translated Python Tests**
         - `pytest commons-cli-python`
         - `pytest commons-csv-python`
     12. **Run GraalVM Glue Code Integration Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
     13. **Run Full Automation Script**
         - `bash run.sh`
         - Ensure script is executable: `chmod +x run.sh`
     14. **Measure Coverage**
         - `python scripts/coverage/cover_local.py`
     15. **Run Glue Automation**
         - `python scripts/generate_glue.py`
         - Output should appear in `generated/commons-cli` and `generated/commons-csv`.
     16. **Collect Clients**
         - `python scripts/clients/selenium.py`
         - `bash scripts/clients/bash_script_version.sh`
     17. **Review and Update Documentation**
         - Update `README.local.md` with system-specific notes (e.g., "Tested on Ubuntu 22.04 x86_64, no GPU").
     18. **Platform-Specific Checks**
         - No GPU: Do not include CUDA/nvidia drivers or references.
         - All shell scripts are Linux-compatible; no Windows-specific instructions needed.
         - Use Linux path separators.
         - All base images and tools must be `amd64`/`x86_64` compatible.
     19. **Final Verification**
         - Repeat running `bash run.sh`, verify all steps on `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`.
     20. **Error Logging and Troubleshooting**
         - Collect logs if any step fails.
         - Confirm all tools installed for x86_64/Ubuntu 22.04.
  **Additional Notes:**
  - **Memory/Storage**: Ensure at least 8GB RAM and >5GB free disk space for GraalVM, Maven builds, and Python environments (review system resources if issues occur).
  - **DOCKER (OPTIONAL)**: If containerizing, use `--platform=linux/amd64` and base images like `ubuntu:22.04` or `python:3.11-slim`. Do not use any ARM or GPU-specific images/tags. Set `WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest` in Dockerfile.

  - The Dockerfile is set up to install all major system dependencies, SDKMAN!, GraalVM Java 17, GraalPython, pyenv, Python 3.11.4, Maven, and a Python virtual environment.

  next step

  - Alternatively, adjust the Dockerfile to handle the absence of `requirements.txt` gracefully (e.g., conditionally copy or skip the install if not present).
  - After resolving the `requirements.txt` issue, rebuild the Docker image and verify that the subsequent steps (dependency installation, script permissions, etc.) execute successfully.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) via SDKMAN!
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) and Python component
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Verify graalpython install
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version"
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Copy requirements.txt if exists (for build-time install, otherwise user will mount/copy)
  COPY requirements.txt $WORKDIR/requirements.txt
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install --upgrade pip && \
      if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 1 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) via SDKMAN!
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) and Python component
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Verify graalpython install
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version"
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:

       - Do not use ARM or other architectures.
     - **SDKMAN!**
       - Tool to install/manage GraalVM.
       - Install per https://sdkman.io/install (works on Ubuntu 22.04).
     - **GraalVM Python Component**
       - Install using `gu install python` after GraalVM is set up.
     - **Maven**
       - Required to build and test Java projects.
       - Use Ubuntu package manager (`apt install maven`) or download from https://maven.apache.org/download.html.
       - Ensure version is compatible with Java 17 (Ubuntu 22.04 default is Maven 3.6+).
     - **Python 3.11.4 (x86_64, Ubuntu)**
       - For running translated Python tests/scripts.
       - Use `pyenv` or official installer (recommended: `pyenv install 3.11.4`).

       - Should come with Python install.
     - **pytest (latest stable)**
       - Install via `pip install pytest`.
     - **Other Python dependencies**
       - Check for requirements.txt or audit scripts, add as needed.
     - **Git**
       - For version control. Install via `sudo apt install git` if needed.
     - **Bash Shell**
       - Native on Ubuntu; all shell scripts will run without issue.

       - Since Docker 28.3.2 is available, optional for containerized builds. Use only amd64-compatible base images (e.g., `ubuntu:22.04`, `python:3.11-slim`, etc.). Do not use any ARM or GPU-specific tags.

     4. **Install Maven**
        - Recommended: `sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install maven`
        - Verify: `mvn -v`
     5. **Install Python 3.11.4**
        - Install pyenv: `curl https://pyenv.run | bash`
        - Install Python: `pyenv install 3.11.4`
        - Set local version: `pyenv local 3.11.4`
        - If pyenv not preferred, use deadsnakes PPA or download from python.org binaries for x86_64.
        - Verify: `python --version`
     6. **Set Up Python Virtual Environment**
        - Run: `python -m venv venv`
        - Activate: `. venv/bin/activate`
        - Verify: Shell prompt shows `(venv)`
     7. **Install Python Dependencies**
        - Update/create `requirements.txt` as needed.
        - Run: `pip install -r requirements.txt`
        - Verify: `pytest --version`
     8. **Clone/Download Project Repository**
        - `git clone <repo-url> /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`
        - Verify folders: `commons-cli`, `commons-csv`, etc.
     9. **Create/Review Configuration Files**
        - Ensure existence and correctness of `.gitignore`, `requirements.txt`, `.env.example`, and `README.local.md`.
     10. **Run Java Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - Verify: All tests pass.
     11. **Run Translated Python Tests**
         - `pytest commons-cli-python`
         - `pytest commons-csv-python`
     12. **Run GraalVM Glue Code Integration Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
     13. **Run Full Automation Script**
         - `bash run.sh`
         - Ensure script is executable: `chmod +x run.sh`
     14. **Measure Coverage**
         - `python scripts/coverage/cover_local.py`
     15. **Run Glue Automation**
         - `python scripts/generate_glue.py`
         - Output should appear in `generated/commons-cli` and `generated/commons-csv`.
     16. **Collect Clients**
         - `python scripts/clients/selenium.py`
         - `bash scripts/clients/bash_script_version.sh`
     17. **Review and Update Documentation**
         - Update `README.local.md` with system-specific notes (e.g., "Tested on Ubuntu 22.04 x86_64, no GPU").
     18. **Platform-Specific Checks**
         - No GPU: Do not include CUDA/nvidia drivers or references.
         - All shell scripts are Linux-compatible; no Windows-specific instructions needed.
         - Use Linux path separators.
         - All base images and tools must be `amd64`/`x86_64` compatible.
     19. **Final Verification**
         - Repeat running `bash run.sh`, verify all steps on `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`.
     20. **Error Logging and Troubleshooting**
         - Collect logs if any step fails.
         - Confirm all tools installed for x86_64/Ubuntu 22.04.

  - **Memory/Storage**: Ensure at least 8GB RAM and >5GB free disk space for GraalVM, Maven builds, and Python environments (review system resources if issues occur).
  - **DOCKER (OPTIONAL)**: If containerizing, use `--platform=linux/amd64` and base images like `ubuntu:22.04` or `python:3.11-slim`. Do not use any ARM or GPU-specific images/tags. Set `WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest` in Dockerfile.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) and Python component via SDKMAN! and gu in a single block
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu && \
      which gu && \
      gu --version && \
      gu install python \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version"
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED: 
     - **GraalVM (Java 17, version 17.0.7-graal, x86_64/amd64 Linux)**
       - Required for glue code integration and GraalPython.
       - Install via SDKMAN! (recommended, works natively on Ubuntu 22.04 x86_64).
       - Do not use ARM or other architectures.
     - **SDKMAN!**
       - Tool to install/manage GraalVM.
       - Install per https://sdkman.io/install (works on Ubuntu 22.04).
     - **GraalVM Python Component**
       - Install using `gu install python` after GraalVM is set up.
     - **Maven**
       - Required to build and test Java projects.
       - Use Ubuntu package manager (`apt install maven`) or download from https://maven.apache.org/download.html.
       - Ensure version is compatible with Java 17 (Ubuntu 22.04 default is Maven 3.6+).
     - **Python 3.11.4 (x86_64, Ubuntu)**
       - For running translated Python tests/scripts.
       - Use `pyenv` or official installer (recommended: `pyenv install 3.11.4`).
     - **pip**
       - Should come with Python install.
     - **pytest (latest stable)**
       - Install via `pip install pytest`.
     - **Other Python dependencies**
       - Check for requirements.txt or audit scripts, add as needed.
     - **Git**
       - For version control. Install via `sudo apt install git` if needed.
     - **Bash Shell**

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) and Python component via SDKMAN! and gu in a single block
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu && \
      which gu && \
      gu --version && \
      gu install python && \
      echo '=== graalvm bin directory ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== graalpython location ===' && which graalpython || true \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install
  RUN bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      which graalpython && graalpython --version"
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) and Python component via SDKMAN! and gu in a single block
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== gu version ===' && gu --version && \
      echo '=== gu list ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== installing graalvm python ===' && gu install python && \
      echo '=== gu list after python ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== graalvm bin directory after python ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME is:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH is:' \$PATH && \
      echo '=== graalpython location ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython || true \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH:' \$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython && \
      \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version \
      "
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

        - Verify: `java -version` (should show GraalVM, version 17.0.7, x86_64)
        - If version not found, use `sdk list java` to choose the closest supported GraalVM 17 x86_64.
     3. **Install GraalVM Python Component**
        - Run: `gu install python`
        - Verify: `graalpython --version`
     4. **Install Maven**
        - Recommended: `sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install maven`
        - Verify: `mvn -v`
     5. **Install Python 3.11.4**
        - Install pyenv: `curl https://pyenv.run | bash`
        - Install Python: `pyenv install 3.11.4`
        - Set local version: `pyenv local 3.11.4`
        - If pyenv not preferred, use deadsnakes PPA or download from python.org binaries for x86_64.
        - Verify: `python --version`
     6. **Set Up Python Virtual Environment**
        - Run: `python -m venv venv`
        - Activate: `. venv/bin/activate`
        - Verify: Shell prompt shows `(venv)`
     7. **Install Python Dependencies**
        - Update/create `requirements.txt` as needed.
        - Run: `pip install -r requirements.txt`
        - Verify: `pytest --version`
     8. **Clone/Download Project Repository**
        - `git clone <repo-url> /home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`
        - Verify folders: `commons-cli`, `commons-csv`, etc.
     9. **Create/Review Configuration Files**
        - Ensure existence and correctness of `.gitignore`, `requirements.txt`, `.env.example`, and `README.local.md`.
     10. **Run Java Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - Verify: All tests pass.
     11. **Run Translated Python Tests**
         - `pytest commons-cli-python`
         - `pytest commons-csv-python`
     12. **Run GraalVM Glue Code Integration Tests**
         - `mvn -f commons-cli-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
         - `mvn -f commons-csv-graal/pom.xml test -Drat.skip`
     13. **Run Full Automation Script**
         - `bash run.sh`
         - Ensure script is executable: `chmod +x run.sh`
     14. **Measure Coverage**
         - `python scripts/coverage/cover_local.py`
     15. **Run Glue Automation**
         - `python scripts/generate_glue.py`
         - Output should appear in `generated/commons-cli` and `generated/commons-csv`.
     16. **Collect Clients**
         - `python scripts/clients/selenium.py`
         - `bash scripts/clients/bash_script_version.sh`
     17. **Review and Update Documentation**
         - Update `README.local.md` with system-specific notes (e.g., "Tested on Ubuntu 22.04 x86_64, no GPU").
     18. **Platform-Specific Checks**
         - No GPU: Do not include CUDA/nvidia drivers or references.
         - All shell scripts are Linux-compatible; no Windows-specific instructions needed.
         - Use Linux path separators.
         - All base images and tools must be `amd64`/`x86_64` compatible.
     19. **Final Verification**
         - Repeat running `bash run.sh`, verify all steps on `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest`.
     20. **Error Logging and Troubleshooting**
         - Collect logs if any step fails.
         - Confirm all tools installed for x86_64/Ubuntu 22.04.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) and Python component via SDKMAN! and gu in a single block
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== gu version ===' && gu --version && \
      echo '=== gu list ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== installing graalvm python ===' && gu install python && \
      echo '=== gu list after python ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== graalvm bin directory after python ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME is:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH is:' \$PATH && \
      echo '=== graalpython location in bin ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython || true && \
      echo '=== graalpython location in languages/python/bin ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython || true && \
      echo '=== languages directory ===' && ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages || true \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install (check both possible locations)
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH:' \$PATH && \
      if [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version; \
      elif [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython --version; \
      else \
          echo 'ERROR: graalpython not found!'; \
          exit 1; \
      fi \
      "
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) via SDKMAN!
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk default java 17.0.7-graal && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== gu version ===' && gu --version && \
      echo '=== gu list ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME is:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH is:' \$PATH \
      "
  # Explicitly install GraalVM Python component with gu in a separate step
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== Installing GraalVM Python ===' && \
      gu install python && \
      echo '=== gu list after python ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== Directory listing after python install ===' && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin || true \
      "
  # Find graalpython binary and log its location
  RUN bash -c " \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      echo '=== Searching for graalpython binary ===' && \
      find \$JAVA_HOME -name graalpython && \
      echo '=== Directory listing of JAVA_HOME ===' && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin || true \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install (check both possible locations and fallback to find result)
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH:' \$PATH && \
      if [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version; \
      elif [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython --version; \
      else \
          GRAALPYTHON_PATH=\$(find \$JAVA_HOME -name graalpython -type f | head -n 1); \
          if [ -x \"\$GRAALPYTHON_PATH\" ]; then \
              echo \"=== Found graalpython at \$GRAALPYTHON_PATH\"; \
              \$GRAALPYTHON_PATH --version; \
          else \
              echo 'ERROR: graalpython not found!'; \
              exit 1; \
          fi; \
      fi \
      "
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk version"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV PATH=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current/bin:$PATH
  # Install GraalVM CE Java 17 via SDKMAN! (use a distribution that supports python component)
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.9-graalce && \
      sdk default java 17.0.9-graalce && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin && \
      echo '=== gu version ===' && gu --version && \
      echo '=== gu list ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME is:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH is:' \$PATH \
      "
  # Explicitly install GraalVM Python component with gu in a separate step, output logs for troubleshooting
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== Installing GraalVM Python ===' && \
      gu install python --verbose 2>&1 | tee /tmp/gu_python_install.log && \
      echo '=== gu list after python ===' && gu list && \
      echo '=== Directory listing after python install ===' && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin || true && \
      echo '=== gu_python_install.log ===' && cat /tmp/gu_python_install.log \
      "
  # Find graalpython binary and log its location
  RUN bash -c " \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      echo '=== Searching for graalpython binary ===' && \
      find \$JAVA_HOME -name graalpython && \
      echo '=== Directory listing of JAVA_HOME ===' && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/bin || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python || true && \
      ls -l \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin || true \
      "
  # Verify graalpython install (check both possible locations and fallback to find result)
  RUN bash -c " \
      source /root/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      export JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current && \
      export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$PATH && \
      echo '=== JAVA_HOME:' \$JAVA_HOME && \
      echo '=== PATH:' \$PATH && \
      if [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version; \
      elif [ -x \"\$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython\" ]; then \
          echo '=== Found graalpython in \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin'; \
          \$JAVA_HOME/languages/python/bin/graalpython --version; \
      else \
          GRAALPYTHON_PATH=\$(find \$JAVA_HOME -name graalpython -type f | head -n 1); \
          if [ -x \"\$GRAALPYTHON_PATH\" ]; then \
              echo \"=== Found graalpython at \$GRAALPYTHON_PATH\"; \
              \$GRAALPYTHON_PATH --version; \
          else \
              echo 'ERROR: graalpython not found!'; \
              echo '=== gu_python_install.log ==='; \
              cat /tmp/gu_python_install.log || true; \
              exit 1; \
          fi; \
      fi \
      "
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/$GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz && \
      ln -s $JAVA_HOME /opt/graalvm
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 9 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/$GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz && \
      ln -s $JAVA_HOME /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List $JAVA_HOME/bin contents before running gu
  RUN ls -l $JAVA_HOME/bin/
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/$GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: Show extraction result before proceeding
  RUN echo /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST && ls -l /opt/ && ls -l /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST/bin/
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/$GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Optionally check extraction result, safer than previous failing RUN
  RUN if [ -d /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST/bin ]; then ls -l /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST/bin/; else ls -l /opt/; exit 1; fi
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 12 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/$GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm $GRAALVM_DIST.tar.gz && \
      ls -l /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List extracted GraalVM directory to verify structure
  RUN ls -lR /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST || (echo "Directory /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST does not exist. Listing /opt:" && ls -l /opt && false)
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 14 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz && \
      ls -l /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List extracted GraalVM directory to verify structure
  RUN ls -l /opt && ls -lR /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST || (echo "Directory /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST does not exist. Listing /opt:" && ls -l /opt && false)
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Copy all project files into the workdir
  COPY . $WORKDIR
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 15 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz && \
      ls -l /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List extracted GraalVM directory to verify structure
  RUN ls -l /opt && ls -lR /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST || (echo "Directory /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST does not exist. Listing /opt:" && ls -l /opt && false)
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Install additional GraalVM Python dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends libz-dev libexpat1 && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GraalVM Updater (gu) Python component with verbose output
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu --verbose install python
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Copy all project files into the workdir
  COPY . $WORKDIR
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz && \
      ls -l /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List extracted GraalVM directory to verify structure
  RUN ls -l /opt && ls -lR /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST || (echo "Directory /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST does not exist. Listing /opt:" && ls -l /opt && false)
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Extra debug: Check gu existence, permissions, and version
  RUN ls -l $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu && $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu --version
  # Extra debug: Show available components before install
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu list
  # Install additional GraalVM Python dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends libz-dev libexpat1 && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Try to install GraalVM Python component, fallback to help if fails
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python || (echo "gu install python failed, showing help:" && $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu --help && false)
  # Verify graalpython is available
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Copy all project files into the workdir
  COPY . $WORKDIR
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 17 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV WORKDIR=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/gluetest
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          git \
          unzip \
          zip \
          wget \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          openssl \
          libssl-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          llvm \
          libncursesw5-dev \
          xz-utils \
          tk-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxmlsec1-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          software-properties-common \
          maven \
          python3-venv \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workdir
  RUN mkdir -p $WORKDIR
  WORKDIR $WORKDIR
  # Install GraalVM Community Edition Java 17 (with Python support) directly from GitHub releases
  ENV GRAALVM_VERSION=22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_DIST=graalvm-ce-java17-22.3.2
  ENV GRAALVM_URL=https://github.com/graalvm/graalvm-ce-builds/releases/download/vm-$GRAALVM_VERSION/graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz
  RUN wget -q $GRAALVM_URL && \
      tar -xzf graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      rm graalvm-ce-java17-linux-amd64-$GRAALVM_VERSION.tar.gz && \
      ln -s /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST /opt/graalvm
  # Debug: List extracted GraalVM directory to verify structure
  RUN ls -l /opt && ls -lR /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST || (echo "Directory /opt/$GRAALVM_DIST does not exist. Listing /opt:" && ls -l /opt && false)
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/opt/$GRAALVM_DIST
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  # Ensure gu is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/gu" ]; then chmod +x $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu; fi
  # Extra debug: Check gu existence, permissions, and version
  RUN ls -l $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu && $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu --version
  # Extra debug: Show available components before install and output to file
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu list | tee /tmp/graalvm_components.txt
  # Install additional GraalVM Python dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends libz-dev libexpat1 && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Print contents of graalvm_components.txt for build log clarity
  RUN cat /tmp/graalvm_components.txt
  # Try to install GraalVM Python component, output error if fails but do NOT stop build
  RUN $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python || (echo "gu install python failed, showing help:" && $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu --help)
  # Verify graalpython is available if installed
  RUN if [ -f "$JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython" ]; then $JAVA_HOME/bin/graalpython --version; else echo "graalpython not available"; fi
  # Install pyenv
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash
  # Install Python 3.11.4 via pyenv
  RUN bash -c "export PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PYENV_ROOT/shims:$PATH && \
      pyenv install 3.11.4 && \
      pyenv global 3.11.4"
  # Set python3 and pip3 symlinks to pyenv Python
  RUN ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /root/.pyenv/versions/3.11.4/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip3
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set up Python virtual environment in the repo
  RUN python3 -m venv venv
  # Install pytest explicitly (redundant if in requirements.txt, but ensures availability)
  RUN . venv/bin/activate && pip install pytest
  # Copy all project files into the workdir
  COPY . $WORKDIR
  # Ensure run.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f run.sh ]; then chmod +x run.sh; fi
  # Default to bash shell
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Entrypoint to interactive shell in workdir
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
